For example, * source folders containing whiley files are (obviously) directly relevant; * however, other containers may be relevant (e.g. if they hold jar files on the * whileypath). * </p> * * <p> * When a resource changes which is relevant to the builder (e.g. a Whiley file, * etc) then the WhileyProject must be notified of this.
